Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐☆

Original: The food was undeniably delicious—flavors were well-balanced, and everything we tried was thoughtfully prepared. The dessert, in particular, stood out as a highlight. However, the portion sizes left much to be desired. I ordered the whole steamed sea bass, and what was served seemed to be barely half of a fish! The steak dish was similarly underwhelming in size. The portion sizes, combined with the cost, detracted somewhat from the overall value of the experience.

Original: A busy spot and would probably be better with reservations. The food here is a little spicy if you can’t handle spice. Reviewer: INKStudios

Date: 2025-05-10

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: WOULD NOT RECOMMEND I'm going to be honest and say that the only reason I'm here was for the free soda. I wouldnt mind leaving a good review....if one was deserved. Our waiter (guy with the dark hair and blond highlights) was incredibly apathetic and terrible when it came to service. He brought us a tray of different dumplings and never told us which was which. We would order and he would forget so we had to ask for things multiple times. He never talked or asked if we needed anything else. He just dumped the food off and left. I told him several times that I was filling out a review for the free soda, to which he acknowledged, and it didn't matter because I was charged for it anyways. The food is honestly overpriced for what was given. It looks great but is mid at best. Overall we just felt unwelcomed the whole time and will not be back.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Kelly Wu

Date: 2025-05-09

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: I had lunch this afternoon at Chi Restaurant & Bar with my family, and it was absolutely amazing. This modern Szechuan restaurant in Manhattan completely exceeded our expectations — both in food and service. The dishes were bursting with bold, authentic Szechuan flavors. We especially loved the spicy chicken, the black truffle beef fried rice, and the lobster — wow, the lobster was perfectly cooked, super flavorful, and just melted in our mouths. Every dish was beautifully presented and full of flavor. Even the family members who don’t usually like spicy food were raving about how good everything was! The interior is gorgeous — modern, stylish, and cozy, with a great atmosphere that makes you want to stay and enjoy every moment. But the real highlight of our experience was our amazing server, Java. She was so professional, kind, and patient. She explained everything on the menu clearly, made spot-on recommendations (which we ended up loving!), and checked on us throughout the meal to make sure we were happy. Her energy was warm and genuine — we felt like she truly cared. We all said how great she was, and we’ll definitely be coming back for her service as much as the food! And right after I left, my friend went to Chi too — they just finished eating and told me they absolutely enjoyed it! They loved the food and said they’ll be coming back for sure. If you’re craving delicious, high-quality Szechuan cuisine in Manhattan with beautiful décor and five-star service, Chi is the spot. Thank you, Java, for making our afternoon so special — we’ll be back soon!

I had lunch this afternoon at Chi Restaurant & Bar with my family, and it was absolutely amazing. This modern Szechuan restaurant in Manhattan completely exceeded our expectations — both in food and service. The dishes were bursting with bold, authentic Szechuan flavors. We especially loved the spicy chicken, the black truffle beef fried rice, and the lobster — wow, the lobster was perfectly cooked, super flavorful, and just melted in our mouths. Every dish was beautifully presented and full of flavor. Even the family members who don’t usually like spicy food were raving about how good everything was! The interior is gorgeous — modern, stylish, and cozy, with a great atmosphere that makes you want to stay and enjoy every moment. But the real highlight of our experience was our amazing server, Java. She was so professional, kind, and patient. She explained everything on the menu clearly, made spot-on recommendations (which we ended up loving!), and checked on us throughout the meal to make sure we were happy. Her energy was warm and genuine — we felt like she truly cared. We all said how great she was, and we’ll definitely be coming back for her service as much as the food! And right after I left, my friend went to Chi too — they just finished eating and told me they absolutely enjoyed it! They loved the food and said they’ll be coming back for sure. If you’re craving delicious, high-quality Szechuan cuisine in Manhattan with beautiful décor and five-star service, Chi is the spot. Thank you, Java, for making our afternoon so special — we’ll be back soon!

But even after we ordered items, such as the happy hour drinks, They gave us different drinks than what we asked for :/ (as our drink orders were no longer available). On top of that we had to keep on asking for a waiter to assist us for essential items such as napkins, and even silverware. Granted, the bartender was completely friendly, And I WISH I could say the SAME ABOUT THE HOST, BUT once we’ve already paid and she saw, I left an under recommended TIP AMOUNT, She came out of the restaurant as we are exiting to ask WHY….. I have never been question about a tip like this before and granted she first went up to the birthday person who I was treating… And it gave us this my card decline 😂 BUT NO, Just wanted to see why we did not give more tip even after it. Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Huijia Lin

Date: 2025-05-07

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: Incredible food on all levels along with creative, beautiful cocktails. We had no misses but particularly loved the pork slice appetizer and the signature braised beef. Flavors are bold and can be quite spicy. They have a large private event room in the back as well. It can be pricey for a large group (plus lots of food served family style), so recommend bringing a group and making a reservation.

Incredible food on all levels along with creative, beautiful cocktails. We had no misses but particularly loved the pork slice appetizer and the signature braised beef. Flavors are bold and can be quite spicy. They have a large private event room in the back as well. It can be pricey for a large group (plus lots of food served family style), so recommend bringing a group and making a reservation.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: James Doty

Date: 2025-05-05

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: We stumbled upon this gem of a Chinese restaurant and left utterly floored. If I could give it six stars, I would. The beef tenderloin with truffle was a revelation—melt-in-your-mouth tender, luxuriously earthy, and seared with such precision it felt like culinary alchemy. The truffle didn’t overpower; it danced in harmony with the beef, adding elegance without stealing the spotlight. Then came the sliced cabbage and pork, which was anything but humble. Smoky, savory, and whispering with umami, it struck that perfect balance between homestyle comfort and elevated flavor. Every bite had crunch, soul, and depth—this dish deserves its own fan club. Before that symphony began, we kicked things off with a mashed eggplant and pepper appetizer that was bright, bold, and addictive. Silky eggplant and punchy pepper created a flavor bomb that lingered just long enough to make you crave the next bite. Service was gracious and efficient, and the ambiance struck a chord—modern, understated, and just refined enough to match the cuisine without being pretentious. Bottom line: This is not your run-of-the-mill takeout spot. It’s a serious culinary experience, rooted in tradition and elevated with just the right touch of flair. We’ll be back—and next time, we’re bringing friends.

We stumbled upon this gem of a Chinese restaurant and left utterly floored. If I could give it six stars, I would. The beef tenderloin with truffle was a revelation—melt-in-your-mouth tender, luxuriously earthy, and seared with such precision it felt like culinary alchemy. The truffle didn’t overpower; it danced in harmony with the beef, adding elegance without stealing the spotlight. Then came the sliced cabbage and pork, which was anything but humble. Smoky, savory, and whispering with umami, it struck that perfect balance between homestyle comfort and elevated flavor. Every bite had crunch, soul, and depth—this dish deserves its own fan club. Before that symphony began, we kicked things off with a mashed eggplant and pepper appetizer that was bright, bold, and addictive. Silky eggplant and punchy pepper created a flavor bomb that lingered just long enough to make you crave the next bite. Service was gracious and efficient, and the ambiance struck a chord—modern, understated, and just refined enough to match the cuisine without being pretentious. Bottom line: This is not your run-of-the-mill takeout spot. It’s a serious culinary experience, rooted in tradition and elevated with just the right touch of flair. We’ll be back—and next time, we’re bringing friends.

Original: If you’re looking for bold, modern Chinese flavors in NYC, Chi Restaurant & Bar in Hell’s Kitchen is the spot. From their perfectly spiced ma-la trio and dimsum platter to the rich truffle beef tenderloin, every dish hits the mark. The sleek, cozy ambiance makes it perfect for date night or dinner with friends. Whether you're a fan of bold spices or just love discovering new foodie gems, Chi hits all the right notes.

If you’re looking for bold, modern Chinese flavors in NYC, Chi Restaurant & Bar in Hell’s Kitchen is the spot. From their perfectly spiced ma-la trio and dimsum platter to the rich truffle beef tenderloin, every dish hits the mark. The sleek, cozy ambiance makes it perfect for date night or dinner with friends. Whether you're a fan of bold spices or just love discovering new foodie gems, Chi hits all the right notes.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Jasmine Henry

Date: 2025-04-30

Stars: ⭐☆☆☆☆

Original: I visited Chi Restaurant and Bar in New York with my partner and two of her colleagues, an important first-time meeting for me. While I covered the bill for our meal, our evening was not yet over. We had planned to continue dining and order additional drinks as a group. However, we were abruptly denied further service by our server, who stated in front of everyone that the tip left on the card was not enough; a humiliating and unprofessional comment made loudly and publicly at our table. What the server didn’t know, and didn’t ask, was that my partner and I had planned to leave an additional cash tip before leaving. I even offered twice to increase the card tip on the spot, but was refused. The server still declined to provide further service. We were left sitting, unable to order anything else, despite our willingness to continue supporting the restaurant and compensate accordingly. To make matters worse, we were seated in an isolated back corner, and the entire interaction gave a clear impression that we were unwelcome. As a woman of color and a tourist, this experience was embarrassing, unnecessary, and disappointing. What should have been a relaxing, social evening turned into an uncomfortable situation that left a lasting impression for all the wrong reasons. Chi Restaurant and Bar must seriously reevaluate its staff training, particularly around professionalism, guest engagement, and cultural sensitivity. No customer should ever be treated with such assumption and disregard.

Reviewer: Mariana Diaz

Date: 2025-03-30

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: From the moment we stepped in, the atmosphere set the stage for an incredible dining experience, perfectly complementing the rich, authentic Chinese flavors. We kicked off our meal with a selection of appetizers that did not disappoint—crispy, flaky green onion pancakes, juicy and flavorful pork soup dumplings (an absolute must-try!), crisp stir-fried string beans, and a refreshing cucumber salad that balanced the bold flavors beautifully. For the main course, we indulged in a feast of expertly prepared dishes. The truffled fried rice was a fragrant, umami-packed delight, while the Chi Signature Braised Short Ribs were melt-in-your-mouth tender, with a deep, savory richness. The spicy cumin lamb delivered just the right amount of heat and aromatics, and the Lao-Gan-Ma General Tso’s Chicken had the perfect crispy texture with a bold, slightly smoky kick. The rice noodles with chicken tied everything together, offering a comforting yet flavorful finish. Every dish was generously portioned and packed with authentic flavors, making this an unforgettable dining experience. Highly recommend!

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Mark “Caveman Cooking” Avery

Date: 2025-03-18

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: Got to NYC with my son to see law schools he's been accepted to, and we were craving some of the city's great Chinese food. Found this place online and it was only a half mile from the hotel. What a find! Walked in, and immediately was taken by the relaxing ambiance and the incredible aromas wafting from the kitchen. Ordered a couple of Chinese beers (Tsing Tao on tap and a bottle of Lucky Buddha) to go along with some Spare Ribs and the Dim Sum sampler (no pic). The former were SO different than the typical ribs you find in Chinese restaurants ... Not boiled and covered in sticky sauce, but slow roasted with flavorful light glaze and served on a stone platter covered with baker's sugar. And the various dim sum were very original and delicious. We still had room for more, so we ordered the Black Truffle Fried Rice with Shredded Duck and the Farmhouse Green Chili Pork Belly (pictured). Both were absolutely phenomenal! Bottom line, this is definitely a restaurant that needs to be on your radar.

Got to NYC with my son to see law schools he's been accepted to, and we were craving some of the city's great Chinese food. Found this place online and it was only a half mile from the hotel. Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Vaida Butkute

Date: 2025-02-24

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐☆

Original: We recently visited Chi Restaurant and had high expectations. The atmosphere was fantastic, and the staff were incredibly friendly, which made for a welcoming experience. We were aware that the prices were on the higher side, so that wasn’t an issue. However, what truly let us down was the food itself. The dishes were overwhelmingly spicy—not just a kick, but to the point of being nearly inedible. While we enjoy spicy food, this was on another level. At first, we thought it might just be us, but we noticed several other tables either refusing to pay or leaving their food untouched. That alone speaks volumes. Overall, a great setting and service, but the food was simply too extreme. A little more balance in the seasoning would make a huge difference.

We recently visited Chi Restaurant and had high expectations. The atmosphere was fantastic, and the staff were incredibly friendly, which made for a welcoming experience. We were aware that the prices were on the higher side, so that wasn’t an issue. However, what truly let us down was the food itself. The dishes were overwhelmingly spicy—not just a kick, but to the point of being nearly inedible. While we enjoy spicy food, this was on another level. At first, we thought it might just be us, but we noticed several other tables either refusing to pay or leaving their food untouched. That alone speaks volumes. Overall, a great setting and service, but the food was simply too extreme. A little more balance in the seasoning would make a huge difference.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Stephen Matlock

Date: 2025-02-19

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐☆

Original: My wife and I came in for dinner around 6:30 pm without a reservation. We found the restaurant through Google. We were greeted, welcomed, and seated almost immediately even though it looked like the entire restaurant and bar were filled We immediately had a waitstaff bring water and menus. We ordered from the American-inspired menu as my wife is used to certain foods, so while i looked longingly at the curry shrimp noodles, we ended up ordering Kung Pao Shrimp, Spicy Cabbage and Pork, and Fried Rice with Chicken. The staff was very accommodating to our dietary needs and made the rice as requested (without egg). The food came within a reasonable amount of time. Given the number of customers and the size of the menu, it was understandable, but even so, it was very fast. The Kung Pao Shrimp was delicious. Sweet and spicy, with jumbo shrimp in the spicy sauce. The Fried Rice with Chicken was tasty also. For me, the standout was the Spicy Cabbage with Pork. The cabbage is very roughly chopped and sauteed in an incredibly flavorful umami sauce with a nice kick of heat (spicier than the Kung Pao Shrimp). The pork appeared to be sliced pork belly with a beautiful unctuous mouth deal from the fatty meat. Stellar meal! The one knock is perhaps due to the popularity and the delightfulness of the food, but the tables are very small, which made it difficult for us to share our food together. I wish I could say 4.5 stars, but Google demands Integer values. A wonderful find in the theatre district!

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Bella Lu

Date: 2025-02-18

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: My recent visit to Chi Restaurant & Bar was nothing short of spectacular. I started with “The Silk Road” mocktail, a refreshing blend of lychee and rose, followed by the “Summer Palace,” which offered a vibrant mix of passion fruit and pineapple. Both drinks were beautifully balanced. The Ma-La Trio was an exciting start to the meal, from the chili-doused poached chicken to the Szechuan peppercorn-infused duck. The Crispy Shrimp Balls were another highlight, perfectly cooked with a delightful spicy aioli and crunchy shredded potatoes. However, the “Birds of a Feather Mao Xue Wang” stole the show. This dish featured two distinct Szechuan chili broths, with meat and vegetables cooked and complemented by the fiery, fragrant sauces. The meal concluded with the Hong Cha Tea Ice Cream, a unique dessert with its rich Chinese black tea ice cream and honey anise caramel. Chi Restaurant & Bar is a must-visit for anyone craving authentic Chinese cuisines with a modern twist. Highly recommended for an immersive and flavorful dining experience!

My recent visit to Chi Restaurant & Bar was nothing short of spectacular. I started with “The Silk Road” mocktail, a refreshing blend of lychee and rose, followed by the “Summer Palace,” which offered a vibrant mix of passion fruit and pineapple. Both drinks were beautifully balanced. The Ma-La Trio was an exciting start to the meal, from the chili-doused poached chicken to the Szechuan peppercorn-infused duck. The Crispy Shrimp Balls were another highlight, perfectly cooked with a delightful spicy aioli and crunchy shredded potatoes. However, the “Birds of a Feather Mao Xue Wang” stole the show. This dish featured two distinct Szechuan chili broths, with meat and vegetables cooked and complemented by the fiery, fragrant sauces. The meal concluded with the Hong Cha Tea Ice Cream, a unique dessert with its rich Chinese black tea ice cream and honey anise caramel. Chi Restaurant & Bar is a must-visit for anyone craving authentic Chinese cuisines with a modern twist. Highly recommended for an immersive and flavorful dining experience!

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Matthew Gantz

Date: 2024-12-01

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: Chi is a fantastic and approachable Chinese restaurant in New York City. They feature unique views on traditional Chinese (real Chinese) food, and they have some classic American Chinese staples too in case you are not adventurous enough. There is lots of Szechuan peppercorn spice, so be prepared. The Ma-La Trio as an appetizer is a great starter, and the Tai Chi Fish Soup was also solid for a group of 5. Pork trotter and sliced beef in chili broth were great as well - great to eat as family style!

Chi is a fantastic and approachable Chinese restaurant in New York City. They feature unique views on traditional Chinese (real Chinese) food, and they have some classic American Chinese staples too in case you are not adventurous enough. There is lots of Szechuan peppercorn spice, so be prepared. The Ma-La Trio as an appetizer is a great starter, and the Tai Chi Fish Soup was also solid for a group of 5. Pork trotter and sliced beef in chili broth were great as well - great to eat as family style!

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Aggie H

Date: 2024-11-10

Stars: ⭐⭐☆☆☆

Original: Had a good lunch experience so decided to go during dinner time. Super crowded & noisy, kitchen was completely overwhelmed that we didn't get our food until 1 hour after we sat. Mala trio was ok, very small portions. The cucumber was nice but the duck was too gamey & the chicken was submerged in chili oil that the edible portion is really negligible. The Chong Qing chicken was extremely salty to the point of inedible. I couldn't wash away the saltiness despite numerous glasses of water. We had to send it back. I'm sure the cook didn't taste it before serving it out, which is quite disappointing given how pricey this place is. The bartender tried very hard to apologize & offered free drinks for the delay. We don't drink but my partner agreed to accept a mocktail, which turned out to be extremely sweet that it's not really pleasant to drink (so we didn't). We ordered string beans, which was tasty. The jasmine rice was dry, which is a sin for an Asian restaurant that claims to offer elevated Chinese cuisine. Unlikely to return for dinner. Maybe it's only good for lunch when there is no crowd so the kitchen can give adequate attention to preparing a decent meal.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Marty Nemec

Date: 2024-09-25

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: I decided to eat here by myself while in NYC. What an absolute treat it was. The restaurant is beautiful. My waitress was kind and attentive, answering all of my questions about what dishes other tables ordered. The presentation of every drink and meal in the whole restaurant were clearly designed to be awe-inspiring. When I spend money at this price point, I always hope my experience will be like what Chi Restaurant and Bar provided me today. First, I ordered the Dragon Paradise cocktail. It is described as having tea, rum, pandan, coconut, yogurt, dairy, and citrus. To me, it tastes like a creamy piña colada with tea in it. It was trippy because the drink is actually see-through but it tastes like it would be a creamy white color. I enjoyed it! Then, I ordered a Szechuan Cucumber Salad as an appetizer and it was so flavorful. It was salty, vinegary, spicy, and more. I honestly would say if you come here, you have to try it. It's that good. My entree was the Truffle Beef Tenderloin, which again, came out with amazing presentation and was so full of flavor. The mushrooms and beef were all coated in a caramelized layer of sweet and salty. There were just enough diced peppers in the dish to keep a welcome spiciness in each bite. I then had fried pumpkin rice cakes and a separate vanilla gelato scoop dessert, which I ate together making the perfect mix of flavors for me. Great meal. Great experience.

Reviewer: TJS

Date: 2024-08-25

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐☆

Original: Not exactly sure what just happened during my two hour dining experience - there are multiple scenarios : 1- the waitress just broke up with her significant other 2- the waitress didn’t appreciate kind, funny, generous customers 3- the waitress had a strong dislike for humanity 4- the waitress was previously a root canal specialist and is applying those people skills to her new found profession Regardless, the outcome is the same. This is quintessential example of how everything else can be spot-on but the lack of friendly staff is a cancer to an organization. Our server (Xinyu M) was top 10 most unfriendly people I’ve ever met in my life - we felt like we were in prison camp. Now for the plus side : I lived in mainland China for many years and this is best Sichuan food I’ve ever had in the US. Insanely good - diverse menu that covers all the bases. Food was authentic and delicious - get the duck in any format … the okra … the xiaolongbao … skip dessert. And don’t ask if they can chop raw ginger into hot water for tea - because apparently ginger is in 50% of their dishes but they can’t accommodate that simple request for 2 people that just spent $300 (it’s my own fault, I asked Xinyu instead of Michael - I should have known 🤦🏼‍♂️… Mr Can Do vs Miss F U) Other servers were very friendly — Michael and others gave service with a smile. Frankly I feel our waitress was judging us for the color of our skin. It was that bad. Atmosphere is nice except for harsh lights over each table - which contributed to the feeling of being trapped in a Sichuan prison with Xinyu M. I did try to express my concerns to the manager on duty but I received a deer in the headlights response (duck in headlights?) so I immediately gave up and brought my commentary here instead of attempting to beat my head against the great wall with zero results. I still left a 25% gratuity because rest of staff (except for the Xinyu and 老板/闆 Manager) were quite friendly and caring - hopefully the staff shares tips 🙄 Worth going? Absolutely! Just make sure you get Michaels section. ❤️🥢🍚🦆🌶️

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Insiya Pardiwala

Date: 2024-08-09

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: Loved this place! The ambience was warm and inviting, perfect for a relaxed meal with friends or family. The service was equally impressive, attentive without being overbearing. We started with the edamame and cucumber salad, both of which were fresh and flavorful. The veggie dumplings were a standout, with a perfectly balanced filling and a light, delicate wrapper. For the main course, we tried the rice noodles, General Tso's chicken, and the green chili chicken with black bean sauce. Each dish was thoughtfully prepared, with distinct flavors that made them memorable. The General Tso's chicken had a perfect blend of sweetness and spice, while the green chili chicken delivered a satisfying kick without overwhelming the taste buds. The highlight of the meal was the dessert—rice cake with lava brown sugar. It was an authentic treat, rich and decadent, yet light enough to leave you wanting more. Overall, this restaurant is a must-visit for anyone looking for quality food in a cozy setting. We will definitely be back to explore more of the menu

Loved this place! The ambience was warm and inviting, perfect for a relaxed meal with friends or family. The service was equally impressive, attentive without being overbearing. We started with the edamame and cucumber salad, both of which were fresh and flavorful. The veggie dumplings were a standout, with a perfectly balanced filling and a light, delicate wrapper. For the main course, we tried the rice noodles, General Tso's chicken, and the green chili chicken with black bean sauce. Each dish was thoughtfully prepared, with distinct flavors that made them memorable. The General Tso's chicken had a perfect blend of sweetness and spice, while the green chili chicken delivered a satisfying kick without overwhelming the taste buds. The highlight of the meal was the dessert—rice cake with lava brown sugar. It was an authentic treat, rich and decadent, yet light enough to leave you wanting more. Overall, this restaurant is a must-visit for anyone looking for quality food in a cozy setting. We will definitely be back to explore more of the menu

Original: Cute restaurant inside. We went at 10:30PM and was surprised to see the place was quite busy at this late. Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Patrick Wong

Date: 2024-02-15

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐☆

Original: TLDR: New popular Sichuan restaurant near Hudson Yards and below Hell's Kitchen. Cool story, a doctor by day and chef by night. Excellent cocktails and a wide variety of food. Fish fillet with chilis was super pretty, the mushrooms with salted egg yolk are addicting and the mala trio is a great way to start! Tried this with a friend and overall pretty tasty. Nice cocktail program with a solid happy hour deal too. We tried the mala trio which was a nice appetizxer dish with three different mala bites. The fish fillets was chopped chilis was a super pretty dish. Double cooked pork was excellent, chongqing chicken was spicy. The mushrooms tossed in salted duck egg yolk was very enjoyable to much on. The dan dan noodle was probably more than we needed but nonetheless, any meal with a mouthful of noodles is happiness. I haven't been back since but I definitely will be. It's gotten much more busy since I came but that's always a good sign.

TLDR: New popular Sichuan restaurant near Hudson Yards and below Hell's Kitchen. Cool story, a doctor by day and chef by night. Excellent cocktails and a wide variety of food. Fish fillet with chilis was super pretty, the mushrooms with salted egg yolk are addicting and the mala trio is a great way to start! Tried this with a friend and overall pretty tasty. Nice cocktail program with a solid happy hour deal too. We tried the mala trio which was a nice appetizxer dish with three different mala bites. The fish fillets was chopped chilis was a super pretty dish. Double cooked pork was excellent, chongqing chicken was spicy. The mushrooms tossed in salted duck egg yolk was very enjoyable to much on. The dan dan noodle was probably more than we needed but nonetheless, any meal with a mouthful of noodles is happiness. I haven't been back since but I definitely will be. It's gotten much more busy since I came but that's always a good sign.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Pavel Yakovlev

Date: 2024-01-05

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: Wife and I ordered ma-la trio appetizer, truffle beef and pork trotters for entree. The food was served rather quickly and it was exceptional, but you have to watch your spice tolerance as ours was tested to the limit with just 2 out of 3 spice/pepper levels for our dishes. Service was top notch and the place was clean, well maintained and appointed. The bill was a bit higher than in many other Asian restaurants, but you do get what you pay for. We did find the menu, which had both authentic and Americanized options, kind of hard to navigate and choose from. We had to ask our waiter to identify the dishes for us by the photos people posted in the reviews. We did discover afterwards though that the on-line menu has photos which help with the identification.

We did discover afterwards though that the on-line menu has photos which help with the identification.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Vicky Lee

Date: 2023-09-21

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: We were super leery of this place (we were afraid it would be like a PF Chang’s style place that caters to non Asians), but we gave it a shot based on reviews and thankfully we did! 4 of us came for a coworker’s birthday dinner, and we had a reservation for 5 pm so the restaurant was mostly empty. All of the food was super good authentic (minus the fried rice since they drizzled truffle oil into it, which was unique and good but definitely not traditional), and my favorite was the boiled fish fillet. Most everything else we got was spicy, so be prepared for the typical Sichuan numbing spices.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Katherine C

Date: 2023-08-25

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: Excellent Szechuan food served in a modern setting. With the recent wave of restaurant openings, I’ve become skeptical of the quality and thought put into new places, especially on the crowded field of Szechuan restaurants in NY—Chi Restaurant exceeds expectations and I’ll be returning for more meals in the future. Our group had several favorite dishes. For appetizers: the dan dan noodles had a hearty, umami-rich flavor and the chili oil wontons were plump and juicy. The cumin lamb was amazingly tender and a standout in terms of presentation. For some interesting dishes, I liked the spicy crispy beef and shimeji mushrooms with salted egg yolk. Both dishes are great if you have a craving for savory, crunchy food. Overall there were no bad dishes in our meal. As we had a fairly large party (10 people), we were offered a private room. Sometimes I dislike booking private rooms as it’s hard to flag down a server, but we received extremely attentive service from staff delivering food, cleaning up dishes between courses, and taking drink orders through the night.

Excellent Szechuan food served in a modern setting. With the recent wave of restaurant openings, I’ve become skeptical of the quality and thought put into new places, especially on the crowded field of Szechuan restaurants in NY—Chi Restaurant exceeds expectations and I’ll be returning for more meals in the future. Our group had several favorite dishes. For appetizers: the dan dan noodles had a hearty, umami-rich flavor and the chili oil wontons were plump and juicy. The cumin lamb was amazingly tender and a standout in terms of presentation. For some interesting dishes, I liked the spicy crispy beef and shimeji mushrooms with salted egg yolk. Both dishes are great if you have a craving for savory, crunchy food. Overall there were no bad dishes in our meal. As we had a fairly large party (10 people), we were offered a private room. Sometimes I dislike booking private rooms as it’s hard to flag down a server, but we received extremely attentive service from staff delivering food, cleaning up dishes between courses, and taking drink orders through the night.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Darrell Loo

Date: 2023-03-13

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: I recently stumbled upon Chi Restaurant through Resy’s newsletter, and as I perused their menu, I knew I had to make a visit. I'm always intrigued by Asian restaurants that are willing to elevate traditional flavors and combine them with a good bar program. So, trying out Chi was both research and pleasure for me. Located in Hell's Kitchen, New York City, Chi 棋 (which means chess in Chinese) is a newly opened restaurant that fully incorporates its theme in the decorations and menu. Chinese idioms related to chess are cleverly used on the menu, adding another layer of fun to the dining experience. Despite it being our third lunch outing, we decided to order quite a few dishes to try. We started with the 将相和, a cold appetizer trio consisting of poached chicken in chili sauce, duck in green vine pepper oil, and cucumber salad. The appetizers were well-prepared with just the right amount of spiciness and flavors, leaving us eager for more. We then moved on to the 滋补汤, a chicken and pork rib soup with ginseng that had a light and delicious broth with a hint of herb from the ginseng. It was quite enjoyable. Next up, we tried the 金字塔的秘密, a steamed pork belly dish that was shaped like a pagoda and stuffed with preserved cabbage and castelvetrano olives (although it's no longer on the menu). The dish was prepared traditionally, and I found it to be quite satisfying. We also had the 干锅藕片, a wok-tossed lotus root with pork belly, and the 咸蛋黄白玉菇, sautéed mushrooms with preserved egg yolk. The lotus root and pork belly were a perfect combination, and I thoroughly enjoyed the savory flavor of the sautéed mushrooms with the preserved egg yolk. My friend ordered the SzeChuan vesper to go with her meal, which consisted of vodka and gin, rice and lillet, five spice chili oil, citrus, and castelvetrano olives. It was a delicious cocktail that complemented her meal perfectly. Overall, our dining experience at Chi was a success, and we truly enjoyed the flavors, presentation, and ambiance of the restaurant.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Olivia

Date: 2023-01-28

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐☆☆

Original: Came in for Lunar New Year's Eve because of the location in Midtown, around 4pm. It was nice and quiet. Clean, new, with designs related to the name (based on Chinese Chess) on the walls. A few private rooms available. The servers were respectful, the tea was good. The potato eggplant pepper dish was good as well. XLB were not bad, a solid choice. Then.... We ordered a chicken dish because another dining group had it and it looked interesting. Alas, it was but a pile of peppers with the smallest bits of chicken scattered throughout, mixed thoroughly and overpoweringly the dried chilies. Difficult to see and hunt for the actual edible bits in the dim lighting. The few morsels we could find were ok, not super delicious for the work to access them. Now, onto the fish; for what is a LNY eve dinner without fish? The most appetizing-sounding was the one with spice, as black bean fish tends to oversweet. Yet this chili fish was also near inedible. Cooked through and presented nicely, yes. Tasty? Not quite. We also had a crab/tofu/bamboo fungus(?) Dish. The special veggies could barely be noticed. Taste was mild, uninspiring. Overall - not worth it. The specialties are inedible and the rest can be found in better quality nearly everywhere else.

Chi Restaurant & Bar

Reviewer: Steve McCoy

Date: 2023-01-09

Stars: ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Original: I have been here 3 times, and the food never disappoints, except the one time I got take out, and I'll get to that! There are essentially two menus: traditional Szechuan offerings, and "American" choices. There is a price difference between the two (the American choices are less expensive). If you want to try something far more authentic, go Szechuan, but be aware that when the item has a "spicy" notation, they mean it! Some items have one chili pepper, or two, or three. One is more than sufficient for my palate! The last time I went (with my wife and son) we had things strictly from the American section of the menu. At a table adjacent to ours, they were served some incredibly amazing dishes (one even incorporated dry-ice, but I don't know what it was. I'll have to ask next time). We got Sesame Chicken, Egg Corn Soup, Eggplant w/ Chinese String Beans, Rice Noodles with Chicken, and Spare Ribs. Everything was amazing, wonderful, and other than the Sesame Chicken didn't come covered with too much sauce. Now, the take out time. I had ordered the spare ribs. When I got them out of the bag at my destination, I discovered they were charred. Not one bit of edible meat on them anywhere. I was glad to see that they had figured that issue out and resolved it! The décor in the space is modern, but yet clearly connected to 'traditional Chinese'. From what we have ben told the owner is a chess player, perhaps of the Grand-Master level. Chess boards are evident in the throughout the space. There are a couple of private rooms with a large table and a large lazy-susan rotating section in the middle. Make a reservation and go. You won't be disappointed!
